* Special Coffee Chat - EDIA Learning Series
<2026-02-04 Wed 12:30>--<2026-02-04 Wed 13:30>
 Understanding Yourself: The first Step in Building Your Inclusivity

When we talk about Introspection, we are speaking to how well we can reflect on and objectively assess the ‘rightness’ of our thoughts and behaviors. Reality is we all make mistakes, take wrong turns, and make bad decisions but the question is: do we recognize, accept and acknowledge it when we do? Think of how many intelligent, high-potential people you know who keep making the same mistakes over and over again. How is it that they don't see the forest for the trees? The culprit here, more often than not, is the human tendency to want to feel right. We want the world to make sense to us so we're driven to interpret information in ways that confirms our preconceptions and biases. Participants will leave this session with a greater ability to reflect on and objectively assess the ‘rightness’ of their thoughts and behaviors.

Please use the Zoom Meeting link below
https://us06web.zoom.us/j/85655325479?pwd=aeKFoFMWOAsaCLI78QHgkJE1hE00Mp.1
Meeting ID: 856 5532 5479
Passcode:014635

* Special Coffee Chat - EDIA Learning Series
<2026-03-11 Wed 12:30>--<2026-03-11 Wed 13:30>
 Understanding Yourself: The first Step in Building Your Inclusivity

When we talk about Introspection, we are speaking to how well we can reflect on and objectively assess the ‘rightness’ of our thoughts and behaviors. Reality is we all make mistakes, take wrong turns, and make bad decisions but the question is: do we recognize, accept and acknowledge it when we do? Think of how many intelligent, high-potential people you know who keep making the same mistakes over and over again. How is it that they don't see the forest for the trees? The culprit here, more often than not, is the human tendency to want to feel right. We want the world to make sense to us so we're driven to interpret information in ways that confirms our preconceptions and biases. Participants will leave this session with a greater ability to reflect on and objectively assess the ‘rightness’ of their thoughts and behaviors.

Please use the Zoom Meeting link below
https://us06web.zoom.us/j/85243315472?pwd=LahKzsmmKsEjYnloqwXAaeGhPGAJxa.1
Meeting ID: 852 4331 5472
Passcode: 430284
